&#151; </B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2021, as compared to the corresponding period of last fiscal year: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT> and increased 38% and 37%, respectively </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

and increased 40% and 38%, respectively </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition section below </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Quarterly Highlights, Product Releases, and Enhancements</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Every quarter Microsoft delivers hundreds of products, either as new releases, services, or enhancements to current products and services. These
releases are a result of significant research and development investments, made over multiple years, designed to help customers be more productive and secure and to deliver differentiated value across the cloud and the edge. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Here are the <U>major product releases and other highlights</U> for the quarter, organized by product categories, to help illustrate how we are
accelerating innovation across our businesses while expanding our market opportunities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Responding to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">At Microsoft, our focus remains on ensuring the safety of our employees, striving to
protect the health and well-being of the communities in which we operate, and providing technology and resources to our customers and partners to help them build resilience and do their best work from anywhere. Additional information about
Microsoft&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> response can be found <U>here</U>. </FONT></P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">To better execute on Microsoft&#146;s mission, we focus our Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) efforts where we can have the most
positive impact. To learn more about our latest initiatives and priorities, please visit our investor relations <U>ESG website</U>.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya
Nadella, chairman and chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Alice Jolla, chief accounting officer, Keith Dolliver, deputy general counsel, and Brett Iversen, general manager of investor relations,
will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <U><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on July&nbsp;27, 2022. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>The India Supreme Court Decision Impact. </I>In March 2021, the India Supreme Court issued a decision on withholding taxes in the case of
Engineering Analysis Centre of Excellence Private Limited vs The Commissioner of Income Tax. Microsoft has historically paid India withholding taxes on software sales through distributor withholding and tax audit assessments in India. The India
Supreme Court ruled favorably for companies in 86 separate appeals, some dating back to 2012, holding that software sales are not subject to India withholding taxes. Although Microsoft was not a party to the appeals, Microsoft&#146;s software sales
in India were determined to be not subject to withholding taxes. Therefore, Microsoft recorded a net income tax benefit of $620&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal year 2021 to reflect the results of the India Supreme Court decision
impacting fiscal year 1996 through fiscal year 2016. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft has provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures related to the India Supreme Court decision to aid investors in better understanding our performance. Microsoft believes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures assist investors by providing additional insight into
its operational performance and help clarify trends affecting its business. For comparability of reporting, management considers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with generally accepted accounting principles
(GAAP) financial results in evaluating business performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial
performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect
of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average
exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as
a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>FOURTH QUARTER FINANCIAL HIGHLIGHTS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SUMMARY </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $8.1&nbsp;billion or 21%, driven by growth across each of our segments. Intelligent Cloud revenue increased driven by Azure.
Productivity and Business Processes revenue increased driven by Office 365 Commercial and LinkedIn. More Personal Computing revenue increased driven by Search advertising. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gross margin increased $6.5&nbsp;billion or 25% driven by growth across each of our segments. Gross margin percentage increased with the change in
estimated useful lives of our server and network equipment. Excluding this impact, gross margin percentage increased despite sales mix shift to cloud, driven by commercial cloud gross margin percentage improvement. Commercial cloud gross margin
percentage increased 4 points to 70% despite revenue mix shift to Azure, driven by improvement across all cloud services on a prior year comparable impacted by strategic investments made to support significant customer engagement and usage in remote
work scenarios. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income increased $5.7&nbsp;billion or 42% driven by growth across each of our segments. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue, gross margin, and operating income included a favorable foreign currency impact of 4%, 5%, and 7%, respectively. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SEGMENT INFORMATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>Productivity and Business Processes </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $2.9&nbsp;billion or 25%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Office Commercial products and cloud services revenue increased $1.5&nbsp;billion or 20%. Office 365
Commercial revenue grew 25% driven by seat growth, up 17% with acceleration in small and medium business and frontline worker offerings, and higher revenue per user. Office Commercial products revenue declined 8% driven by continued customer shift
to cloud offerings, on a low prior year comparable impacted by a slowdown in transactional licensing. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

Microsoft 365 Consumer subscription revenue, on a low prior year comparable impacted by a slowdown in transactional licensing. Microsoft 365 Consumer subscribers increased 22% to 51.9&nbsp;million. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

advertising demand in our Marketing Solutions business, up 97%, and an improving job market in our Talent Solutions business. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>OTHER INCOME, NET </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Other income, net was $310&nbsp;million driven by interest and dividends income and net gains on investments, offset in part by interest expense.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>INCOME TAXES </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The current quarter effective tax rate was 15% compared to 17% in the prior year. The decrease in our effective tax rate was primarily due to tax
benefits from an agreement between the U.S. and China related to transfer pricing and tax benefits from the conclusion of a foreign tax audit. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>REMAINING PERFORMANCE OBLIGATIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue allocated to remaining performance obligations, which includes
unearned revenue and amounts that will be invoiced and recognized as revenue in future periods, was $146&nbsp;billion as of June&nbsp;30, 2021, of which $141&nbsp;billion is related to the commercial portion of revenue. We expect to recognize
approximately&nbsp;50% of this revenue over the next&nbsp;12&nbsp;months and the remainder thereafter. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>
